[2018-12-09 07:19:21]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT id,name,office_email FROM cms_employees WHERE id =15 AND is_active = 1


[2018-12-09 07:19:21]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT id,name FROM cms_clients WHERE is_active = 1


[2018-12-09 07:19:21]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1


[2018-12-09 07:19:22]

SELECT count(token) as token_count  FROM cms_emp_login_sessions WHERE token	= '03293db0a67871ad036730841905cf98'


[2018-12-09 07:19:23]
Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-09 07:19:23]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id

				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query
 Param Details:

[2018-12-09 08:55:54]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-09 09:10:59]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

						, approvals

						, date_format(created_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as created_date
						, created_by

					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = '18-0000004'

Function Details: db_query
 Param Details:

[2018-12-09 09:17:24]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment

				, cms_outbound_document.amount

				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name

Function Details: get_doc_primary_no 
 Param Details : 
"outbound_no cms_outbound_document"


[2018-12-09 10:03:23]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT IFNULL( CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  LPAD(  SUBSTRING_INDEX(MAX(outbound_no),'-',-1) + 1 ,7,'0000000')), CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-','0000001')) AS outbound_no  FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE YEAR(created_date) = YEAR(NOW()) ORDER BY outbound_no desc limit 0,1

Function Details: db_query

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list

SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content

				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks

				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

                                        LEFT JOIN cms_master_list ON cms_outbound_document.ctg_id = cms_master_list.id
                                        LEFT JOIN cms_employees ON cms_outbound_document.created_by = cms_employees.id WHERE outbound_no='18-0000001'

 Param Details:

[2018-12-09 11:13:51]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT id,name FROM cms_clients WHERE is_active = 1


[2018-12-09 11:13:51]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-09 11:13:53]
Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-09 11:13:53]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

						  outbound_no		
						, date_format(outbound_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as outbound_date	
						, client_id
						, attention_to
						, email_content
						, email
						, attachment
						, remarks
						, approvals
						, status_id
						, ctg_id
						, amount
						, notes
						, is_active
						, date_format(created_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as created_date
						, created_by
						, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name			
					 FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = '18-0000001'

				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL

                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name

                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

Function Details: get_doc_primary_no 
 Param Details : 
"outbound_no cms_outbound_document"


[2018-12-09 11:26:58]
Function Details: db_query
 Param Details: 
SELECT IFNULL( CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-',  LPAD(  SUBSTRING_INDEX(MAX(outbound_no),'-',-1) + 1 ,7,'0000000')), CONCAT( RIGHT(YEAR(NOW()),2),'-','0000001')) AS outbound_no  FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE YEAR(created_date) = YEAR(NOW()) ORDER BY outbound_no desc limit 0,1

[2018-12-09 11:26:58]
Function Details: db_query

SELECT count(*) as id_count FROM cms_outbound_document WHERE outbound_no = '18-0000002'

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-12-09 11:32:24]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                           FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                           WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                           UNION ALL
                           SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                           cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                           FROM
                           cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                           WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details:

[2018-12-09 16:00:29]
Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

									FROM cms_employees
									LEFT JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

 Param Details :

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT group_concat(office_email SEPARATOR ';') as email
									FROM cms_employees
									INNER JOIN cms_employees_access ON cms_employees.id =  cms_employees_access.emp_id
									WHERE cms_employees_access.module_id = 17 AND verify_it = 1 AND approve_it = 1 AND cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list

[2018-12-09 16:05:58]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10
